This add-on adds a symbol to compact and expand the message header plane. The compact header view mode can be set to either one or two lines.\n\nA customization dialog can be opened for the toolbar in the header pane (right mouse button context menu) to change the displayed buttons and their style.\n\nThe shortcut \"SHIFT+h\" can be used to toggle between expanded and compact header view.\n\nThis add-on integrates the functionality of \"RSS Linkify Subject\" by Alex Dedul (<a href=\"https://addons.mozilla.org/en-US/thunderbird/addon/1704)\" rel=\"nofollow\">https://addons.mozilla.org/en-US/thunderbird/addon/1704)</a>.\n\nThere is also an option to display only the email addresses in the compact header view. Of course there are third party services, that help you to send newsletters; but you have to trust them.\n\nMail Merge solves these problems by creating individual messages for each recipient from a draft message - locally on your computer without the need to trust third party services!\n\n\n----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n<strong>Step by Step:</strong> (Address Book)\nScreenshots: <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205597.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Draft Message</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205598.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Draft Message</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205599.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Draft Message</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205618.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Mail Merge Dialog</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205624.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Preview Message Dialog</a>\n<ol><li>Create a New Message (\"File -&gt; New -&gt; Message\")</li><li>Add the Recipients to To or add the Variable(s) to To, e.g.: <em>{{PrimaryEmail}}</em> or <em>{{FirstName}} {{LastName}} &lt;{{PrimaryEmail}}&gt;</em></li><li>Add other Recipients to Cc (optional) (variables are supported)</li><li>Add other Recipients to Bcc (optional) (variables are supported)</li><li>Add the Subject (variables are supported)</li><li>Add the Body (variables are supported)</li><li>Add (global) Attachments (optional)</li><li>Click \"File -&gt; Mail Merge\"</li><li>Select \"Address Book\" and check \"Deliver Mode\"</li><li>Add (individual) Attachments (optional) (variables are supported)</li><li>Check \"Start\", \"Stop\" and \"Pause\" (optional)</li><li>Click \"OK\"</li></ol>The Draft Message is saved as Template in your Current Account and for each Recipient a New Message is automagically saved in your Outbox (\"Local Folders -&gt; Outbox\"). Ready for Delivery: \"File -&gt; Send Unsent Messages\"\n\n\n<strong>Step by Step:</strong> (CardBook)\nScreenshots: <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205597.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Draft Message</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205602.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Draft Message</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205603.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Draft Message</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205617.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Mail Merge Dialog</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205624.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Preview Message Dialog</a>\n<ol><li>Create a New Message (\"File -&gt; New -&gt; Message\")</li><li>Add the Recipients to To or add the Variable(s) to To, e.g.: <em>{{email}}</em> or <em>{{firstname}} {{lastname}} &lt;{{email}}&gt;</em></li><li>Add other Recipients to Cc (optional) (variables are supported)</li><li>Add other Recipients to Bcc (optional) (variables are supported)</li><li>Add the Subject (variables are supported)</li><li>Add the Body (variables are supported)</li><li>Add (global) Attachments (optional)</li><li>Click \"File -&gt; Mail Merge\"</li><li>Select \"CardBook\" and check \"Deliver Mode\"</li><li>Add (individual) Attachments (optional) (variables are supported)</li><li>Check \"Start\", \"Stop\" and \"Pause\" (optional)</li><li>Click \"OK\"</li></ol>The Draft Message is saved as Template in your Current Account and for each Recipient a New Message is automagically saved in your Outbox (\"Local Folders -&gt; Outbox\"). Ready for Delivery: \"File -&gt; Send Unsent Messages\"\n\n\n<strong>Step by Step:</strong> (CSV)\nScreenshots: <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205600.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Draft Message</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205601.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Draft Message</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205619.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Mail Merge Dialog</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205623.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Preview File Dialog</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205624.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Preview Message Dialog</a>\n<ol><li>Create a New Message (\"File -&gt; New -&gt; Message\")</li><li>Add the Variable(s) to To, e.g.: <em>{{Email}}</em> or <em>{{FirstName}} {{LastName}} &lt;{{Email}}&gt;</em></li><li>Add other Recipients to Cc (optional) (variables are supported)</li><li>Add other Recipients to Bcc (optional) (variables are supported)</li><li>Add the Subject (variables are supported)</li><li>Add the Body (variables are supported)</li><li>Add (global) Attachments (optional)</li><li>Click \"File -&gt; Mail Merge\"</li><li>Select \"CSV\" as \"Source\" and check \"Deliver Mode\"</li><li>Add (individual) Attachments (optional) (variables are supported)</li><li>Select the \"File\" and check \"Character Set\", \"Field Delimiter\" and \"Text Delimiter\"</li><li>Check \"Start\", \"Stop\" and \"Pause\" (optional)</li><li>Click \"OK\"</li></ol>The Draft Message is saved as Template in your Current Account and for each Recipient a New Message is automagically saved in your Outbox (\"Local Folders -&gt; Outbox\"). Ready for Delivery: \"File -&gt; Send Unsent Messages\"\n\n\n<strong>Step by Step:</strong> (JSON)\nScreenshots: <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205600.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Draft Message</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205601.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Draft Message</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205620.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Mail Merge Dialog</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205623.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Preview File Dialog</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205624.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Preview Message Dialog</a>\n<ol><li>Create a New Message (\"File -&gt; New -&gt; Message\")</li><li>Add the Variable(s) to To, e.g.: <em>{{Email}}</em> or <em>{{FirstName}} {{LastName}} &lt;{{Email}}&gt;</em></li><li>Add other Recipients to Cc (optional) (variables are supported)</li><li>Add other Recipients to Bcc (optional) (variables are supported)</li><li>Add the Subject (variables are supported)</li><li>Add the Body (variables are supported)</li><li>Add (global) Attachments (optional)</li><li>Click \"File -&gt; Mail Merge\"</li><li>Select \"JSON\" as \"Source\" and check \"Deliver Mode\"</li><li>Add (individual) Attachments (optional) (variables are supported)</li><li>Select the \"File\"</li><li>Check \"Start\", \"Stop\" and \"Pause\" (optional)</li><li>Click \"OK\"</li></ol>The Draft Message is saved as Template in your Current Account and for each Recipient a New Message is automagically saved in your Outbox (\"Local Folders -&gt; Outbox\"). Ready for Delivery: \"File -&gt; Send Unsent Messages\"\n\n\n<strong>Step by Step:</strong> (Spreadsheet)\nScreenshots: <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205600.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Draft Message</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205601.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Draft Message</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205621.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Mail Merge Dialog</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205623.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Preview File Dialog</a> | <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205624.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Preview Message Dialog</a>\n<ol><li>Create a New Message (\"File -&gt; New -&gt; Message\")</li><li>Add the Variable(s) to To, e.g.: <em>{{Email}}</em> or <em>{{FirstName}} {{LastName}} &lt;{{Email}}&gt;</em></li><li>Add other Recipients to Cc (optional) (variables are supported)</li><li>Add other Recipients to Bcc (optional) (variables are supported)</li><li>Add the Subject (variables are supported)</li><li>Add the Body (variables are supported)</li><li>Add (global) Attachments (optional)</li><li>Click \"File -&gt; Mail Merge\"</li><li>Select \"Spreadsheet\" as \"Source\" and check \"Deliver Mode\"</li><li>Add (individual) Attachments (optional) (variables are supported)</li><li>Select the \"File\" and check \"Sheet Name\"</li><li>Check \"Start\", \"Stop\" and \"Pause\" (optional)</li><li>Click \"OK\"</li></ol>The Draft Message is saved as a Template in your Current Account and for each Recipient a New Message is automagically saved in your Outbox (\"Local Folders -&gt; Outbox\"). Ready for Delivery: \"File -&gt; Send Unsent Messages\"\n\n\n----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n<strong>Tutorials:</strong> (External)\n\nChris Bryson has published two videos:\n<a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=l8aOcsojVEo\" rel=\"nofollow\">How to Mail Merge with Thunderbird</a>\n<a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=mcwJuyt_xnM\" rel=\"nofollow\">Mail Merge Attachments with Thunderbird Email</a>\n\nRaffael Herrmann has published a guide (German):\n<a href=\"https://code-bude.net/2016/11/04/serienmails-mit-thunderbird-erstellen/\" rel=\"nofollow\">Serienmails mit Thunderbird erstellen</a>\n\n\n----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n<strong>Deliver Mode:</strong>\nMail Merge supports \"Save as Draft\", \"Send Later\" (default) and \"Send Now\"  as \"Deliver Mode\" for the individual and personalized messages.\n\n<strong>Use \"Send Now\" as \"Deliver Mode\" at your own risk!</strong>\nIt is strongly recommended to use \"Send Later\" as \"Deliver Mode\" and to check the individual and personalized messages in the folder \"Local Folders -&gt; Outbox\". Bugs in Thunderbird, bugs in Mail Merge and bugs in other add-ons may lead to unexpected and undesired results.\n\n\n----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n<strong>Attachments:</strong> (Global)\nGlobal Attachments, i.e. attachments that are the same for every recipient, can be added normally using the toolbarbutton \"Attach\".\n\n\n<strong>Attachments:</strong> (Individual)\nIndividual Attachments, i.e. attachments that are different for every recipient, can be added in the \"Attachments\" field in the Mail Merge Dialog, e.g.:\n<code>{{Attachment}}</code>\n<code>C:\\Path\\To\\File\\{{Attachment}}</code>\n\nMultiple (individual) attachments can be separated by line breaks, e.g.:\n<code>C:\\Path\\To\\File\\{{Attachment1}}\nC:\\Path\\To\\File\\{{Attachment2}}\nC:\\Path\\To\\File\\{{Attachment3}}</code>\n\n\n----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n<strong>CSV:</strong>\n<a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Comma-separated_values\" rel=\"nofollow\">Comma-separated values</a>\n<code>records are separated by line breaks (\\r, \\n, \\r\\n)\nfields are separated by field delimiters (comma, semicolon, colon, tab)\nfields may be enclosed within text delimiters (double quote, single quote, none)\nfields with embedded line breaks must be enclosed within text delimiters\nfields with embedded field delimiters must be enclosed within text delimiters\nfields with embedded text delimiters must be enclosed within text delimiters\nembedded text delimiters must be doubled\nfirst record must contain column names</code>\n\n\n<strong>CSV:</strong> (Example)\n<code>FirstName,LastName,Gender,Email,Attachment\nJohn,Doe,m,john.doe@example.com,C:\\MyFile.pdf</code>\n\n\n<strong>Character Set:</strong> (Recommendation)\n<a href=\"https://encoding.spec.whatwg.org/\" rel=\"nofollow\">Character Sets Supported by Thunderbird</a>\n<em>windows-1252</em> (Windows)\n<em>utf-8</em> (Linux &amp; Mac)\n\n\n----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n<strong>JSON:</strong> (Array of Arrays)\nMail Merge supports UTF-8 encoded files in JSON format with Array of Arrays.\n\n<strong>JSON:</strong> (Array of Arrays) (Example)\n<code>[\n[\"FirstName\",\"LastName\",\"Gender\",\"Email\",\"Attachment\"],\n[\"John\",\"Doe\",\"m\",\"john.doe@example.com\",\"C:\\\\MyFile.pdf\"]\n]</code>\n\n\n----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n<strong>Spreadsheet:</strong>\nSupport for spreadsheets is based on <a href=\"https://sheetjs.com/\" rel=\"nofollow\">SheetJS</a>. See: <a href=\"https://github.com/sheetjs/js-xlsx#file-formats\" rel=\"nofollow\">File Formats supported by SheetJS</a>\n\n\n----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n<strong>Batch:</strong> (Start, Stop and Pause)\n<em>Start</em>: Number of the First Message (optional)\n<em>Stop</em>: Number of the Last Message (optional)\n<em>Pause</em>: Pause between Messages in Seconds (optional) (variables are supported)\n\n\n<strong>Pause:</strong> (Advanced)\nThe \"Pause\" field supports fixed and random pauses as well as variables, e.g.:\nFixed Pause: <em>10</em> (Pause 10 seconds)\nRandom Pause: <em>10-60</em> (Pause between 10 and 60 seconds)\nVariables: <em>{{Pause}}</em>\n\n\n----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n<strong>Send Later:</strong>\nMail Merge supports <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/addon/send-later-3\" rel=\"nofollow\">Send Later</a>:\n<a href=\"http://blog.kamens.us/send-later#mailmerge\" rel=\"nofollow\">User Guide</a>\n\n\n----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n<strong>Line Breaks:</strong>\nThunderbird uses an HTML editor internally. You can create line breaks with &lt;br&gt;.\n\n\n<strong>Links and Images:</strong>\nThunderbird uses an HTML editor internally. You can create (individual) links and (individual) images with \"Insert -&gt; HTML\", e.g.:\nLink: <em>&lt;a href=\"{{link}}\"&gt;</em>\nImage: <em>&lt;img src=\"{{image}}\"&gt;</em>\n\n\n----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n<strong>Preview File Dialog:</strong>\nScreenshot: <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205623.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Preview File Dialog</a>\nThe \"Preview File Dialog\" offers you the chance to briefly check the file, i.e. CSV, JSON or Spreadsheet. <strong>It is no adequate compensation for inspecting the files themselves!</strong>\n\n\n<strong>Preview Message Dialog:</strong>\nScreenshot: <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205624.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Preview Message Dialog</a>\nThe \"Preview Message Dialog\" offers you the chance to briefly check the messages. <strong>It is no adequate compensation for inspecting the individual and personalized messages themselves!</strong>\n\n\n----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n<strong>Deliver Mode Warning</strong>\nScreenshot: <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205632.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Deliver Mode Warning</a>\n<strong>Use \"Send Now\" as \"Deliver Mode\" at your own risk!</strong>\nIt is strongly recommended to use \"Send Later\" as \"Deliver Mode\" and to check the individual and personalized messages in the folder \"Local Folders -&gt; Outbox\". Bugs in Thunderbird, bugs in Mail Merge and bugs in other add-ons may lead to unexpected and undesired results.\n\n\n<strong>Recipients Reminder:</strong>\nScreenshot: <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205625.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Recipients Reminder</a>\nThe \"Recipients Reminder\" shall prevent accidentally clicking on \"Send Now\" or \"Send Later\". To start Mail Merge please click \"Cancel\" and use the menu \"File -&gt; Mail Merge\" or the toolbarbutton \"Mail Merge\". The \"Recipients Reminder\" can be activated and deactivated in the Mail Merge Options (\"Tools -&gt; Add-ons Preferences -&gt; Mail Merge\"). Threshold: <em>extensions.mailmerge.recipients</em>\n\n\n<strong>Variables Reminder:</strong>\nScreenshot: <a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/user-media/previews/full/205/205626.png\" rel=\"nofollow\">Variables Reminder</a>\nThe \"Variables Reminder\" shall prevent accidentally clicking on \"Send Now\" or \"Send Later\". To start Mail Merge please click \"Cancel\" and use the menu \"File -&gt; Mail Merge\" or the toolbarbutton \"Mail Merge\". The \"Variables Reminder\" can be activated and deactivated in the Mail Merge Options (\"Tools -&gt; Add-ons Preferences -&gt; Mail Merge\").\n\n\n----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n<strong>Variable:</strong> <em>{{name}}</em>\nThe variable will be replaced by the value of the field <em>name</em>, e.g.:\n<em>{{FirstName}}</em>: the variable will be replaced by the value of the field <em>FirstName</em>\n<em>{{LastName}}</em>: the variable will be replaced by the value of the field <em>LastName</em>\n<em>{{PrimaryEmail}}</em>: the variable will be replaced by the value of the field <em>PrimaryEmail</em>\n\n<strong>Variable:</strong> <em>{{name|if|then}}</em>\nIf the value of the field <em>name</em> equals <em>if</em>, then the variable will be replaced by <em>then</em>.\n\n<strong>Variable:</strong> <em>{{name|if|then|else}}</em>\nIf the value of the field <em>name</em> equals <em>if</em>, then the variable will be replaced by <em>then</em>, else by <em>else</em>.\n\n\n<strong>Variable:</strong> <em>{{name|*|if|then|else}}</em> (includes)\nIf the value of the field <em>name</em> <em>includes</em> <em>if</em>, then the variable will be replaced by <em>then</em>, else by <em>else</em>.\n\n<strong>Variable:</strong> <em>{{name|^|if|then|else}}</em> (starts with)\nIf the value of the field <em>name</em> <em>starts with</em> <em>if</em>, then the variable will be replaced by <em>then</em>, else by <em>else</em>.\n\n<strong>Variable:</strong> <em>{{name|$|if|then|else}}</em> (ends with)\nIf the value of the field <em>name</em> <em>ends with</em> <em>if</em>, then the variable will be replaced by <em>then</em>, else by <em>else</em>.\n\n\n<strong>Variable:</strong> <em>{{name|==|if|then|else}}</em> (equal to) (number)\nIf the value of the field <em>name</em> is <em>equal to</em> <em>if</em>, then the variable will be replaced by <em>then</em>, else by <em>else</em>.\n\n<strong>Variable:</strong> <em>{{name|&gt;|if|then|else}}</em> (greater than) (number)\nIf the value of the field <em>name</em> is <em>greater than</em> <em>if</em>, then the variable will be replaced by <em>then</em>, else by <em>else</em>.\n\n<strong>Variable:</strong> <em>{{name|&gt;=|if|then|else}}</em> (greater than or equal to) (number)\nIf the value of the field <em>name</em> is <em>greater than or equal to</em> <em>if</em>, then the variable will be replaced by <em>then</em>, else by <em>else</em>.\n\n<strong>Variable:</strong> <em>{{name|&lt;|if|then|else}}</em> (less than) (number)\nIf the value of the field <em>name</em> is <em>less than</em> <em>if</em>, then the variable will be replaced by <em>then</em>, else by <em>else</em>.\n\n<strong>Variable:</strong> <em>{{name|&lt;=|if|then|else}}</em> (less than or equal to) (number)\nIf the value of the field <em>name</em> is <em>less than or equal to</em> <em>if</em>, then the variable will be replaced by <em>then</em>, else by <em>else</em>.\n\n\n<strong>Nested Variables:</strong>\nVariables can be nested. For example: To create individual emails only for your premium customers, you can add something like this in the To field:\n{{Premium|x|{{Email}}}}\n\n\n<strong>Warning:</strong> (Variables in the From / To / Cc / Bcc / Reply fields)\nAdvanced variables like \"includes\", \"starts with\" and \"ends with\" as well as the \"numbers\" may not work as expected in the From / To / Cc / Bcc / Reply fields!\n\n\n----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n<strong>Address Book:</strong>\n<a href=\"https://dxr.mozilla.org/comm-central/source/comm/mailnews/addrbook/public/nsIAbCard.idl\" rel=\"nofollow\">Addressbook Properties Supported by Thunderbird</a>\n<code><em>{{FirstName}}</em>\n<em>{{LastName}}</em>\n<em>{{DisplayName}}</em>\n<em>{{NickName}}</em>\n<em>{{PrimaryEmail}}</em>\n<em>{{SpouseName}}</em>\n<em>{{FamilyName}}</em>\n<em>{{SecondEmail}}</em>\n<em>{{HomeAddress}}</em>\n<em>{{HomeAddress2}}</em>\n<em>{{HomeCity}}</em>\n<em>{{HomeState}}</em>\n<em>{{HomeZipCode}}</em>\n<em>{{HomeCountry}}</em>\n<em>{{WebPage2}}</em>\n<em>{{WorkAddress}}</em>\n<em>{{WorkAddress2}}</em>\n<em>{{WorkCity}}</em>\n<em>{{WorkState}}</em>\n<em>{{WorkZipCode}}</em>\n<em>{{WorkCountry}}</em>\n<em>{{WebPage1}}</em>\n<em>{{HomePhone}}</em>\n<em>{{WorkPhone}}</em>\n<em>{{FaxNumber}}</em>\n<em>{{PagerNumber}}</em>\n<em>{{CellularNumber}}</em>\n<em>{{JobTitle}}</em>\n<em>{{Department}}</em>\n<em>{{Company}}</em>\n<em>{{Custom1}}</em>\n<em>{{Custom2}}</em>\n<em>{{Custom3}}</em>\n<em>{{Custom4}}</em>\n<em>{{Notes}}</em>\n<em>{{AnniversaryYear}}</em>\n<em>{{AnniversaryMonth}}</em>\n<em>{{AnniversaryDay}}</em>\n<em>{{BirthYear}}</em>\n<em>{{BirthMonth}}</em>\n<em>{{BirthDay}}</em>\n<em>{{_AimScreenName}}</em>\n<em>{{_GoogleTalk}}</em>\n<em>{{_Yahoo}}</em>\n<em>{{_Skype}}</em>\n<em>{{_QQ}}</em>\n<em>{{_MSN}}</em>\n<em>{{_ICQ}}</em>\n<em>{{_JabberId}}</em>\n<em>{{_IRC}}</em></code>\n\n\n<strong>Address Book:</strong>\n<a href=\"https://freeshell.de/~kaosmos/morecols-en.html\" rel=\"nofollow\">MoreFunctionsForAddressBook</a>\n<code><em>{{MFFABcustom1}}</em>\n<em>{{MFFABcustom2}}</em>\n<em>{{MFFABcustom3}}</em>\n<em>{{MFFABcustom4}}</em>\n<em>{{MFFABcustom5}}</em>\n<em>{{MFFABcustom6}}</em>\n<em>{{MFFABcustom7}}</em>\n<em>{{MFFABcustom8}}</em>\n<em>{{MFFABcustom9}}</em>\n<em>{{MFFABcustom10}}</em>\n<em>{{MFFABemail1}}</em>\n<em>{{MFFABemail2}}</em>\n<em>{{MFFABemail3}}</em>\n<em>{{MFFABemail4}}</em>\n<em>{{MFFABemail5}}</em></code>\n\n\n<strong>Address Book:</strong>\n<a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/addon/gcontactsync/\" rel=\"nofollow\">gContactSync</a>\n<code><em>{{ThirdEmail}}</em>\n<em>{{FourthEmail}}</em>\n<em>{{HomeFaxNumber}}</em>\n<em>{{OtherNumber}}</em>\n<em>{{PrimaryEmailType}}</em>\n<em>{{SecondEmailType}}</em>\n<em>{{ThirdEmailType}}</em>\n<em>{{FourthEmailType}}</em>\n<em>{{WorkPhoneType}}</em>\n<em>{{HomePhoneType}}</em>\n<em>{{FaxNumberType}}</em>\n<em>{{CellularNumberType}}</em>\n<em>{{PagerNumberType}}</em>\n<em>{{HomeFaxNumberType}}</em>\n<em>{{OtherNumberType}}</em>\n<em>{{WebPage1Type}}</em>\n<em>{{WebPage2Type}}</em>\n<em>{{Relation0}}</em>\n<em>{{Relation1}}</em>\n<em>{{Relation2}}</em>\n<em>{{Relation3}}</em>\n<em>{{Relation4}}</em>\n<em>{{Relation5}}</em>\n<em>{{Relation0Type}}</em>\n<em>{{Relation1Type}}</em>\n<em>{{Relation2Type}}</em>\n<em>{{Relation3Type}}</em>\n<em>{{Relation4Type}}</em>\n<em>{{Relation5Type}}</em></code>\n\n\n----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n<strong>CardBook:</strong>\n<a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/addon/cardbook/\" rel=\"nofollow\">CardBook</a>\n<code><em>{{dirPrefId}}</em>\n<em>{{cardurl}}</em>\n<em>{{etag}}</em>\n<em>{{updated}}</em>\n<em>{{deleted}}</em>\n<em>{{created}}</em>\n<em>{{lastname}}</em>\n<em>{{firstname}}</em>\n<em>{{othername}}</em>\n<em>{{prefixname}}</em>\n<em>{{suffixname}}</em>\n<em>{{fn}}</em>\n<em>{{nickname}}</em>\n<em>{{bday}}</em>\n<em>{{gender}}</em>\n<em>{{adr}}</em>\n<em>{{tel}}</em>\n<em>{{email}}</em>\n<em>{{mailer}}</em>\n<em>{{tz}}</em>\n<em>{{geo}}</em>\n<em>{{title}}</em>\n<em>{{role}}</em>\n<em>{{agent}}</em>\n<em>{{org}}</em>\n<em>{{categories}}</em>\n<em>{{note}}</em>\n<em>{{prodid}}</em>\n<em>{{sortstring}}</em>\n<em>{{uid}}</em>\n<em>{{rev}}</em>\n<em>{{url}}</em>\n<em>{{version}}</em>\n<em>{{class1}}</em>\n<em>{{key}}</em>\n<em>{{impp}}</em>\n<em>{{others}}</em>\n<em>{{photo}}</em>\n<em>{{value}}</em>\n<em>{{localURI}}</em>\n<em>{{URI}}</em>\n<em>{{extension}}</em>\n<em>{{logo}}</em>\n<em>{{value}}</em>\n<em>{{localURI}}</em>\n<em>{{URI}}</em>\n<em>{{extension}}</em>\n<em>{{sound}}</em>\n<em>{{value}}</em>\n<em>{{localURI}}</em>\n<em>{{URI}}</em>\n<em>{{extension}}</em>\n<em>{{kind}}</em>\n<em>{{member}}</em>\n<em>{{dispn}}</em>\n<em>{{dispadr}}</em>\n<em>{{disphomeadr}}</em>\n<em>{{dispworkadr}}</em>\n<em>{{disptel}}</em>\n<em>{{disphometel}}</em>\n<em>{{dispworktel}}</em>\n<em>{{dispcelltel}}</em>\n<em>{{dispemail}}</em>\n<em>{{disphomeemail}}</em>\n<em>{{dispworkemail}}</em>\n<em>{{dispimpp}}</em>\n<em>{{dispurl}}</em>\n<em>{{pgname}}</em>\n<em>{{pg}}</em></code>\n\n\n<strong>CardBook:</strong> (Address)\n<a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/addon/cardbook/\" rel=\"nofollow\">CardBook</a>\n<code><em> {{adr}}</em>\n<em>{{adrpostoffice}}</em>\n<em>{{adrextended}}</em>\n<em>{{adrstreet}}</em>\n<em>{{adrlocality}}</em>\n<em>{{adrregion}}</em>\n<em>{{adrpostalcode}}</em>\n<em>{{adrcountry}}</em></code>\n\n\n<strong>CardBook:</strong> (Types)\n<a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/addon/cardbook/\" rel=\"nofollow\">CardBook</a>\nThe configured \"Types\" in the \"CardBook Preferences\" can be used by its \"Code\" as a first parameter for the properties address, email, impp, phone and url. For example:\n<code><em>{{adr#home}}</em>\n<em>{{adr#work}}</em>\n<em>{{email#home}}</em>\n<em>{{email#work}}</em>\n<em>{{impp#home}}</em>\n<em>{{impp#work}}</em>\n<em>{{tel#cell}}</em>\n<em>{{tel#fax}}</em>\n<em>{{tel#home}}</em>\n<em>{{tel#work}}</em>\n<em>{{url#home}}</em>\n<em>{{url#work}}</em></code>\n\nIn case you have multiple entries, you can use a number as a second parameter for the properties address, email, impp, phone and url. For example:\n<code><em>{{url#home#0}}</em>\n<em>{{url#home#1}}</em>\n<em>{{url#home#2}}</em></code>\n\n\n<strong>CardBook:</strong> (Custom Fields)\n<a href=\"https://addons.thunderbird.net/addon/cardbook/\" rel=\"nofollow\">CardBook</a>\nThe configured \"Custom Fields\" in the \"CardBook Preferences\" can be used by its \"Field Name\". For example:\n<code><em>{{others#X-CUSTOM1}}</em>\n<em>{{others#X-CUSTOM2}}</em>\n<em>{{others#X-CUSTOM3}}</em>\n<em>{{others#X-CUSTOM4}}</em></code>\n\n\n----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n<strong>Custom Headers:</strong>\nMail Merge supports <a href=\"http://kb.mozillazine.org/Custom_headers\" rel=\"nofollow\">Custom Headers</a>: I think they do this in error, and also reported this to Microsoft, but unfortunately they haven't changed their policy yet.\n\nIf you run into issues with an email provider not supporting redirection of messages, please contact them and see if you can make them change their policy. You can point them to this add-on, <a href=\"https://bugzil.la/12916\" title=\"Bug 12916 - Allow bounce/redirect of mail messages\" rel=\"nofollow\">bug 12916</a>, or <a href=\"https://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2822.txt\" rel=\"nofollow\">RFC2822</a> section 3.6.6.\n\nAs a workaround you can also redirect your messages through another email provider, e.g. Gmail, but this Posta Elettronica Certificata (PEC) nasce per sostituire il servizio di posta raccomandata nella comunicazione tra i professionisti, i cittadini e le istituzioni rendendo più efficiente il meccanismo di comunicazione. Il sistema, basandosi sullo standard S/MIME, certifica lo scambio di documenti tra il mittente e il destinatario della comunicazione e informa automaticamente il mittente sullo stato della comunicazione fornendo ricevute che hanno valenza legale.\n\nThunderPEC si propone come strumento per la gestione semplificata della posta elettronica certificata in Thunderbird e può essere abilitato selettivamente sui soli account PEC.\n\nUn messaggio di posta elettronica certificata è costituito da una Busta di Trasporto che contiene il messaggio di posta elettronica originale inviato dal mittente ed un allegato XML che riassume i dati della transazione. La busta di trasporto è firmata digitalmente dal gestore PEC sorgente. \n\nThunderPEC visualizza direttamente il messaggio di posta elettronica originale e offre gli strumenti per poter operare sul messaggio originale. Inoltre, gestisce le notifiche PEC inviate dai gestori PEC coinvolti nella transazione. \n\nThunderPEC semplifica la gestione delle <b>notifiche PEC</b> e delle <b>ricevute <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://outgoing.prod.mozaws.net/v1/a3c6fc477c3d56c1ce635eb5e5c9cea47e41f6749e6fc96bf12e54828b4d5dc3/https%3A//it.wikipedia.org/wiki/Processo_civile_telematico_%2528diritto_italiano%2529\">PCT</a> e FatturaPA</b>, attraverso la funzionalità <b>Stato del messaggio</b> che permette di avere una visione di insieme/riassuntiva delle notifiche associate ad un messaggio inviato.\n\nThunderPEC introduce <b>tre filtri rapidi (Messaggi, Notifiche, 53/94)</b> che permettono la selezione rapida dei soli messaggi PEC, delle sole notifiche PEC o dei messaggi PEC conenenti notifiche secondo la Legge 53/94.\n\nThunderPEC  implementa, inoltre, le seguenti funzionalità:\n<ul><li><b>Archiviazione delle notifiche PEC e ricevute PCT/FatturaPA</b> che offre la possibilità di salvare le notifiche PEC associate ad un messaggio, le ricevute PCT/FatturaPA ed il messaggio stesso all'interno di un file zip per l'archiviazione.</li><li><b>Cerca PA</b> per ricercare l'indirizzo PEC di un ufficio pubblico sull'infrastruttura Open Data di DigitPA (<a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://outgoing.prod.mozaws.net/v1/9d934bb98932984ad82f8b8826247a60b2de29421d8a6297c988ad8f1b63e1a6/http%3A//spcdata.digitpa.gov.it\">spcdata.digitpa.gov.it</a>).</li><li><b>Trasferisci Account</b> per trasferire i dati di un account PEC da <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://outgoing.prod.mozaws.net/v1/ea007840c341b208b928e4cf637e3f81a4cf22ab9f398d24e6f638cd10e8c30a/http%3A//youtu.be/uuN8pQqERek\">ThunderPEC a PocketPEC</a>.</li></ul>\nThunderPEC introduce, all'interno del menu principale, il menu ThunderPEC, composto da:\n1) <b>Account</b>: per la gestione degli account PEC.\n1.a) <b>Aggiungi</b>: per aggiungere un nuovo account PEC. Cliquez sur le lien ci-dessus :-)</b>\n\nThunderbird Conversations est une extension pour Thunderbird qui comme son nom l'indique affiche vos courriers en mode conversation. Les fonctions les plus sympas sont les suivantes :\n- la vue en conversation classique qui récupère les messages de tous les dossiers, à la manière de Gmail ;\n- l'intégration de <a href=\"https://addons.mozilla.org/en-US/thunderbird/addon/243985/\" rel=\"nofollow\">Thunderbird Contacts</a> : les participants sont repérables par une infobulle, qui comprend leur avatar et profil de Facebook, Twitter…\n- la réponse rapide, avec l'autocomplétion qui vous permet de dire votre mot dans une discussion en un clin d'œil\n- les citations masquées qui améliorent la lisibilité\n- les raccourcis-clavier,\n- et quelques astuces supplémentaires à découvrir.","en-US":"<a href=\"https://github.com/protz/thunderbird-conversations/wiki\" rel=\"nofollow\"><b>Website</b> (including documentation)</a> - <a href=\"https://github.com/protz/thunderbird-conversations/wiki/FAQ\" rel=\"nofollow\">FAQ</a> - <a href=\"https://github.com/protz/thunderbird-conversations/issues\" rel=\"nofollow\">Report bugs</a> - <a href=\"https://github.com/protz/thunderbird-conversations/commits/master\" rel=\"nofollow\">Track changes</a>\n\nThunderbird Conversations is a Thunderbird extension which, as the name implies, enables a conversation view in your Thunderbird. Notable features include:\n<ul><li>a regular conversation view that fetches messages from all folders, and behaves just like Gmail’s</li><li>a quick reply feature, with autocomplete, that allows you to reply to a thread in a snap,</li><li>quoted parts are collapsed,</li><li>keyboard shortcuts,</li><li>and a few other bonus features.</li></ul>\n<b>Don't forget to hit View &gt; Sort By &gt; Threaded</b> in the menus. To remove the unified folder view, hit <b>View &gt; Folders &gt; All</b>.\n\n\n<b>We welcome feedback, but only if you've read the <b><a href=\"https://github.com/protz/thunderbird-conversations/wiki/faq\" rel=\"nofollow\">FAQ</a></b> before :-)</b>\n\n<b>Known Issues with Thunderbird 68</b>\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"https://github.com/protz/thunderbird-conversations/issues/1361\" rel=\"nofollow\">Quick Reply is not working in 68</a>.
